[Part II—Sec. 2
NOTIFICATIONS  BY  GOVERNMENT
ANIMAL HUSBANDRY DAIRYING AND FISHERIES
DEPARTMENT.
Election for Electing Members to formation of Committee
for Tamil Nadu State Veterinary Council under the
Indian Veterinary Council Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 324, Animal Husbandry Dairying and
Fisheries (AH-3), 16th December 2013,
Margazhi 1, Vijaya,  Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2044.]
No.II(2)/AHDF/66/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by sub-rule (1) of rule 3 of the Tamil Nadu State Veterinary
Council Rules, 2004 the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby calls
upon the persons entered in the State Veterinary register for
the purpose specified therein.
S. VIJAYAKUMAR,
 Secretary to Government.
HIGHWAYS AND MINOR PORTS DEPARTMENT
Acquisition of Lands
[G.O. (D) No. 265, Highways and Minor Ports (HQ2),
27th December 2013,
Margazhi 12, Vijaya, Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2044.]
No. II(2)/HWMP/67/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule
below have to be acquired for Highways purpose for the
formation of IT Corridor Expressway (Phase II) by improving
the Old Mahabalipuram Road to six lane and it having already
been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be
awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled
(or) managed by The Chief Engineer (C & M), Highways
Department after considering the cause shown by the owner
or other person having interest on such lands, as the case
may be, do hereby publish the following notice under
sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways
Act 2001. (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires lands specified in the schedule
below and measuring to an extent of 46170 sq.mts of Rayatwari
dry lands to the same, a little more or less required in
Thandalam Village, Chengalpattu Taluk, Kancheepuram District
for the formation of IT Corridor Expressway (Phase II) by
improving the Old Mahabalipuram Road to six lane in
Kancheepuram District.
The plan of the lands are is kept in the office of the Special
Tahsildar, Land Acquisition Radial Road Scheme, Tambaram
and may be inspected at any time during office hours.
SCHEDULE
Kancheepuram District, Chengalpattu (Now Thiruporur) Taluk,
114. Thandalam Village.

No. II (2)/HWMP/68/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule
below have to be acquired for Highways purpose to wit for
Nagapattinam District, Sirkali Taluk, Vilamthidasamuthiram
Village –Acquisition of  Rayot Manai and dry lands to an extent
of 597  Sq. mtrs  in Vilanthirdasamuthiram Village for the
formation of approaches to road Over Bridge at 128/8 of
abandoned National Highways 45A- Villupuram-Puduchery
Cuddalore-Nagapattinam Road including reconstruction of small
bridges at Km 129/4, 131/2, 132/6, 133/6  and 133/8 retaining
wall under Comprehensive Road in Infrastructure Development
Programme (CRIDP) 2010-2011 in favour of Highways
Department and it has already been decided that the entire
amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be
paid out of the funds controlled and managed by Divisional
Engineer (Highways), Nagapattinam after considering the cause
shown by the owner (or) other person having interest on such
lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following
Notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE.
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the
Schedule below measuring  to an extent of 597 Sq.mters
in Vilandhidasamuthiram Village in Sirkali Taluk,
Nagapattinam District to the same a little more or less required
for the formation of approaches to Road Over Bridge at
128/8 of abandoned National Highways 45A – Villupuram –
Puduchery Cuddalore- Nagapattinam Road including
reconstruction of small bridges at Km 129/4, 131/2, 132/6,
133/6 and 133/8 retaining wall under the Comprehensive Road
Infrastructure Development Programme (CRIDP) 2010-2011.
The Plan  of the land/lands is kept in the office of Divisional
Engineer, Highways, Nagapattinam/ Tahsildar Sirkali and may
be inspected at any time during office hours.

No.II (2)/HWMP/70/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule
below have to be acquired for highways to wit for the formation
of Vandalur to Walajabad Road to extend the old road as four
lane in Survey No. 33/4B situated in 149. Serapanacheri Village,
Sriperumbudur Taluk, Kancheepuram District and it already
been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be
awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled
and managed by Chief Engineer (Construction and Maintenance)
Highways Department and having considered the cause shown
by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands
as the case may be do hereby published the following notice
under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways
Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways
Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor of
Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the dry lands specified in the
Schedule below measuring to an extent of 1325 Sq. mts. to
the same, a little more or less required of the purpose of
widening and strengthening the Vandalur to Walajabad Road
in 149. Serapanacheri Village, Sriperumbudur Taluk,
Kancheepuram District.
The plan of the land is kept in the office of the District
Revenue Officer, Sriperumbudur and may be inspected at any
time during office hours.

No. II(2)/HWMP/75/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having  satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below
have to be acquired for Highways Purpose for providing
approach road to the bridge at Keezhakarai Village, Kattumannar
Kovil Taluk , Cuddalore District,  and it  has already  been
decided that the  entire  amount  of compensation to be
awarded for the land is to be paid out of the funds controlled
and managed by Divisional Engineer (H),  Projects, Cuddalore,
after  Considering the  cause shown by the owner or
other person having interest on such lands, as the  case
may be, do hereby publish  the following  notice
under 
sub-section 
(1) 
of 
Section 
15
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001  (Tamil Nadu
Act 34/2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the wet lands specified in the
schedule below Measuring to  an extent of 0.11.0 hectares to
the same, a little more or less required for  providing approach
road to the bridge in Chidambaram-Trichy road at Keezhakarai
Village, Kattumannar Kovil Taluk in Cuddalore District.
The plan of the land is kept in the Office of the Revenue
Divisional Officer, Chidambaram  and may be inspected at
any time during office hours.

No. II(2)/HWMP/76/2014.—The Government of Tamil Nadu
having satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below
have to be acquired for highways Purpose  to wit for the
“Construction of Road Over Bridge in lieu of  existing Railway
Level Crossing  No.228 situated between Kattur-Lalgudi Railway
Stations (Lalgudi Town)” and it having already been decided
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the
lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed
by Divisional Engineer (Highways) Tiruchirappalli, after
considering the cause shown by the owner or other person
having interest on such land as the case may be do hereby
Publish the following Notice under sub-Section (1) of
Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu
Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor
of Tamilnadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule
below Measuring to  an extent of 2525 Square Meters of Ryot
manai and dry lands in Siruthaiyur Village, Lalgudi Taluk,
Tiruchirappalli District to  the same, a little more or less needed
for Highways Purpose for the Construction of Road Over Bridge
in lieu of existing Railway Level Crossing No.228 situated
between Kattur-Lalgudi Railway Stations (Lalgudi Town) in
Tiruchirappalli District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the Office of the District
Collector, Tiruchirappalli and may be inspected at any time
during office hours.

in the Schedule below  measuring to an extent of 77 Square

6.04.0
[G.O (D) No. 293, Highways and Minor Ports (HP1),
31st December 2013, Margazhi 16, Vijaya, Thiruvalluvar
 Aandu-2044.]
No. II(2)/HWMP/82/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule
below  have to be acquired for Highways purpose  to wit
for the formation of approaches to Road Over Bridge  at
128/8 of abandoned  National Highways 45A – Villupuram –
Puduchery – Cuddalore – Nagapattinam Road including
reconstruction of small bridges at   Km 129/4, 131/2, 132/6
and 133/6,133/8 retaining wall under Comprehensive Road
Infrastructure Development Programme (CRIDP) 2010-2011 in
favour of Highways Department and it has already been decided
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the
lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed
by Divisional Engineer (Highways), Nagapattinam after
considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby
publish the following Notice under Sub-Section (1) of Section
15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act
34 of 2002).
NOTICE
  Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the
schedule below measuring to an extent of 2251 Sq.mtrs in
Vilandhidasamuthiram  village in Sirkali Taluk, Nagapattinam
District to the same, a little more or less required for the
formation of approaches to Road Over Bridge  at 128/8 of
abandoned National Highways 45A - Villupuram - Puduchery -
Cuddalore - Nagapattinam Road including reconstruction of
small bridges at Km 129/4, 131/2,132/6 and 133/6, 133/8
retaining wall under the Comprehensive Road Infrastructure
Development Programme (CRIDP) 2010-2011.
The Plan of the land/lands is kept in the office of the
Divisional Engineer, Highways, Nagapattinam/ Tahsildar, Srikali
and may be inspected at any time during office hours.


Feb. 5, 2014]

[G.O (D) No. 294, Highways and Minor Ports (HS1),
31st 
December 
2013, 
Margazhi 
16, 
Vijaya,
Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2044.]
No. II(2)/HWMP/83/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the Lands specified in the Schedule
below are required for the purpose of Construction of Road
over Bridge in lieu of existing Level Crossing No. 366 at Railway
Km. 496/16-497/1 at Madurai District, Madurai South Taluk,
Palanganatham  between Madurai Junction and
Thirupparankundram Railway Station and it having already been
decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded
for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and
managed by the Divisional Engineer (NABARD and Rural
Roads), Highways Department, Madurai and after having
considered the cause shown by the owner or other persons
having interest in the said lands, as the case may be, do hereby
publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section
15 of Tamil Nadu, Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act
34/2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways
Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002) the Governor of Tamil Nadu
hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below
measuring to an extent of 0.2849.0 Sq. mts. in Madakulam
Village, Madurai South Taluk, Madurai District to the same, a
little more or less required for the purpose of Construction of
Road over Bridge in lieu of existing Level Crossing
No. 366 at Railway Km. 496/16-497/1 at Palanganatham between
Madurai Junction and Thirupparankundram Railway Station.
The plan of the land is kept in the office of the Revenue
Divisional Officer, Madurai. 20 and may be inspected at any
time during office hours.

[G.O (D) No. 295, Highways and Minor Ports (HP1),
31st December 2013, Margazhi 16, Vijaya Thiruvalluvar
 Aandu-2044.]
No. II(2)/HWMP/84/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule
below  have to be acquired for Highways purpose  to wit for
the formation of approaches to the Road Over Bridge at
Km ¼ on the Vellaiyaur in Seruthur Velanganni Salai in
Nagapattinam District under Tsunami Rehabilitation
Programme and it having already been decided that the
entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands
is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by
Divisional Engineer (Highways), Nagapattinam after considering
the cause shown by the owner (or) other person having interest
on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the
following Notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the dry and Rayot manavari
lands specified in the Schedule below  measuring to an extent
of 0.3555 hectares lands in Prathabharamapuram Village and
0.03.0 hectares in Vellaganni village, in Kilvelur Taluk,
Nagapattinam District to the same , a little more or less required
for the formation of approaches to the Road Over Bridge at
Km ¼ on the Vellaiyaur in Seruthur Vellanganni Salai in
Nagapattinam District under Tsunami Rehabilitation Programme.
The Plan of the Land/Lands are kept in the office of the
Tahsildar, Kilvelur and may be inspected at any time during
office hours.

[G.O (D) No. 296, Highways and Minor Ports (HP2),
31st December 2013, Margazhi 16, Vijaya, Thiruvalluvar
 Aandu-2044.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/85/2014.-The Governor of Tamil Nadu having
satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have
to be acquired for highways purpose for “the Construction of
Mannachanallur Bye-Pass Road from KM 2/2 to KM 4/6 of
Trichy-Thuraiyur Road (SH62)” and it having already been
decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded
for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and
managed by Divisional Engineer (Highways) Tiruchirappalli, after
considering the cause shown by the owner or other person
having interest on such lands as the case may be. The
following notice is issued under sub-Section (1) of section 15
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act
34/2002)
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Govenor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the
Schedule below measuring to an extent of 7.30.0 Hectares to
the same, a little more or less needed for public purpose for
“the Construction of Mannachanallur By Pass Road from KM
2/2 to KM 4/6 of Trichy-Thuraiyur Road (SH62)”. in Tiruchirappalli
District.
The Plan of the lands is kept in the Office of the District
Collector, Tiruchirappalli and may be inspected at any time
during office hours.

HOME DEPARTMENT
Secretariat, 5th February 2014.
Messers Paazee Forex Trading India Private Limited,
Tiruppur District Under the Tamil Nadu Protection of
Interests of Depositors (in Financial Establishments Act.
No.II(2)/HO/94/2014.—
[Tamil Nadu Protection of Interests of Depositors (in Financial
Establishments) Act, 1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 44 of 1997) -
Messers Paazee Forex Trading India Private Limited, Tiruppur
District - Default in return of deposits by the Financial
Establishment - Ad-Interim order attaching the movable properties
of the said Financial Establishment under section 3 of the said
Act - Orders - Issued.]
The following Government order is republished:—
[G.O. Ms. No.13, Home (Police XIX), 3rd  January 2014,
ñ£˜èN 19, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´ 2044.]
READ:
1. G.O. Ms. No.324, Home dated 20-5-2013.
2. G.O. Ms. No. 1012, Home dated 26-11-2013.
READ ALSO:-
From the Superintendent of Police, Central Bureau of
Investigation, Economic Offences Wing-II, Chennai, Letter
No.RC/12/E/2011/2974, dated 07-10-2013.
Order: No.13, Home (Police XIX), 3rd January 2014.)
WHEREAS, complaints have been received from a number
of depositors that Messers Paazee Forex Trading India Private
Limited, Tiruppur District financial establishment has defaulted
the return of deposits made by the depositors after maturity;
AND Whereas, the Government are satisfied that the said
financial establishment is not likely to return the deposits to
the depositors and hence, the Government have to protect the
interests of such depositors;
AND Whereas, proposal for attachment of properties worth
Rs.4,49,69,000/- were earlier identified and Government have
issued ad-interim order attaching the properties of the said
financial establishment vide Government order first read above.
AND Whereas, the movable properties specified in the
Schedule to this order are alleged to have been procured by
the said financial establishment from and out of the deposits
collected from the depositors;
NOW, Therefore, in exercise of the powers conferred by
section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Protection of Interests of Depositors
(in Financial Establishments) Act, 1997 (Tamil Nadu Act, 44
of 1997), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby makes an ad-
interim order attaching the movable properties standing in the
names of the partners of Messers Paazee Forex Trading India
Private Limited, Tiruppur District and other person specified in
the Schedule to this order and transfers the control over the
said movable properties to the Competent Authority, namely,
the Competent Authority and District Revenue Officer, Tiruppur
District appointed under the said Act.
2. The Competent Authority, and District Revenue Officer,
Tiruppur District is requested to pursue further action in
accordance with the procedure laid down in sub-sections (3)
and (4) of section 4 of the said Act and also the formalities
prescribed in the Tamil Nadu Protection of Interests of Depositors
(in Financial Establishments) Rules, 1997.
3.
The Special Public Prosecutor, Special Court for the
Tamil Nadu Protection of Interests of Depositors (in Financial
Establishments) Act, 1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 44 of 1944)
Coimbatore is requested to render necessary assistance to the
Competent Authority for filing the application before the said
Special Court.
(By Order of The Governor)


Feb. 5, 2014]

No. II(2)/HOU/95/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by clause (a) of sub-section (1) of Section 23 of the Tamil
Nadu Buildings (Lease and Rent Control) Act, 1960 (Tamil Nadu
Act 18 of 1960), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby makes

LABOUR AND EMPLOYMENT DEPARTMENT.
Notifications under the Employees, State Insurance Act.
Exemption from the Tamil Nadu Asbesto, Alangulam,
operation of Virudhunagar, for certain period under the
Act.
[G.O.(D) No. 588, Labour and Employment (L1), 14th November
2013, äŠðC 28, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´ 2044.]
No. II(2)/LE/96/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 87 read with section 91A of the Employees’ State
Insurance Act, 1948 (Central Act XXXIV of 1948), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby exempts the Tamil Nadu Asbestos,
Alangulam, Virudhunagar District from the operation of the said
Act for the period from 14-11-2013 to 13-11-2014.
(1) The above exemption is subject to the following conditions,
namely:-
(a)
The aforesaid factory wherein the employees are
employed shall maintain a Register showing the
names and designations of the exempted
employees.
(b)
Notwithstanding the exemption, the employees shall
continue to receive such benefits under the said
Act to which they might have become entitled to
on the basis of the contributions paid prior to the
date from which exemption granted by this
Notification operates.
(c) The contribution for the exempted period, if already
paid shall not be refunded.
(2) The employer of the said factory shall submit in respect
of the period during which that factory was subject to the
operation of the said Act (hereinafter referred to as “the said
period”) returns in such form and containing such particulars
as were due from it in respect of the said period under the
Employees State Insurance (General) Regulations, 1950.
(3) Any Social Security Officer appointed by the Corporation
under sub-section (1) of Section 45-A of the said Act, or other
official authorised in this behalf shall, for the purpose of,-
(i)
Verifying the particulars contained in any return
submitted under sub-section (1) of Section 44 of
the said Act for the said period ; or
(ii)
ascertaining whether registers and records were
maintained as required by the Employees State
Insurance (General) Regulations, 1950 for the said
period; or
(iii)
ascertaining whether the employees continues to
be entitled to the benefits provided by the employer
in cash and in kind, being benefits in consideration
of which exemption is being granted under this
Notification; or
(iv)
ascertaining whether any of the provisions of the
said Act had been complied with during the period
when such provisions were in force in relation to
the said factory be empowered to,-
(a) require the principal or immediate employer to furnish
to him such information as he may consider necessary; or
(b) enter any Corporation, office or other premises occupied
by such principal or immediate employer at any reasonable time
and require any person found in charge thereof to produce to
such Social Security Officer or other official and allow him to
examine such documents, books and other documents relating
to the employment of persons and payment of wages or to
furnish to him such information as he may consider
necessary ; or
(c) examine the principal or immediate employer, his agent
or servant, or any person found in such factory, establishment
office or other premises, or any person when the said Social
Security Officer or other official has reasonable cause to believe
to have been an employee; or
(d) make copies of or take extracts from any register,
account book or other document maintained in such factory,
office or other premises.
Exemption from the Development Consultants Private
Limited, Chennai for certain periold under the Act.
[G.O. (D) No. 657, Labour and Employment (L1), 19th December
2013, ñ£˜èN 4, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2044.]
No. II(2)/LE/97/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 88 read with section 91-A of the Employees’ State
Insurance Act, 1948 (Central Act XXXIV of 1948), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby exempts the Development Consultants


Feb. 5, 2014]

151

(b)

continue to receive such benefits under the said

Regulations, 1950.
(3) Any Social Security Officer appointed by the Corporation
under sub-section (1) of Section 45 of the said Act, or other
official authorised in this behalf shall, for the purpose of,-
(i)
Verifying the particulars contained in any return
submitted under sub-section (1) of Section 44 of
the said Act for the said period ; or
(ii)
ascertaining whether registers and records were
maintained as required by the Employees State
Insurance (General) Regulations, 1950 for the said
period; or
(iii) ascertaining whether the employees continues to be
entitled to the benefits provided by the employer in
cash and in kind, being benefits in consideration
of which exemption is being granted under this
Notification; or
(iv)
ascertaining whether any of the provisions of the
said Act had been complied with during the period
when such provisions were in force in relation to
the said workshops and stores be empowered to,-
(a) require the principal or immediate employer to furnish
to him such information as he may consider necessary; or
(b) enter any management, office or other premises occupied
by such principal or immediate employer at any reasonable time
and require any person found in charge thereof to produce to
such Social Security Officer or other official and allow him to
examine such documents, books and other documents relating
to the employment of persons and payment of wages or to
furnish to him such information as he may consider
necessary ; or
(c) examine the principal or immediate employer, his agent
or servant, or any person found in such management office
or other premises, or any person when the said Social Security
Officer or other official has reasonable cause to believe to have
been an employee; or
(d) make copies of or take extracts from any register,
account book or other document maintained in such
management office or other premises.
Exemption from the Permanent and Temporary Employees
of Christian Medical College and Hospital, Vellore for
certain period under the Act.
[G.O.(D) No. 703, Labour and Employment (L1), 31st December
2013, Margazhi 16, Vijaya, Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2044.]
No. II(2)/LE/98/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 87 read with section 91-A of the Employees’ State
Insurance Act, 1948 (Central Act XXXIV of 1948), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby exempts the Permanent and Temporary
Employees of Christian Medical College and Hospital, Vellore
from the operation of the said Act for the period from 1-1-2014
to 31-12-2014.
(1) The above exemption is subject to the following conditions,
namely:-
(a)
The aforesaid management wherein the employees
are employed shall maintain a Register showing the
names and designations of the exempted
employees.
(b)
Notwithstanding the exemption, the employees shall
continue to receive such benefits under the said
Act to which they might have become entitled to
on the basis of the contributions paid prior to the
date from which exemption granted by this
Notification operates.
(c)
The contribution for the exempted period, if already
paid shall not be refunded.
(2) The employer of the said Management shall submit in
respect of the period during which that Management was
subject to the operation of the said Act (hereinafter referred
to as “the said period”) returns in such form and containing
such particulars as were due from it in respect of the said
period under the Employees State Insurance (General)
Regulations, 1950.
(3) Any Social Security Officer appointed by the Corporation
under sub-section (1) of Section 45 of the said Act, or other
official authorised in this behalf shall, for the purpose of,-
(i)
Verifying the particulars contained in any return
submitted under sub-section (1) of Section 44 of
the said Act for the said period ; or
(ii)
ascertaining whether registers and records were
maintained as required by the Employees State
Insurance (General) Regulations, 1950 for the said
period; or
(iii)
ascertaining whether the employees continue to be
entitled to the benefits provided by the employer in
cash and in kind, being benefits in consideration
of which exemption is being granted under this
Notification; or

Notification No. II(2)/LE/277/2010, published on pages 251 and
252 of Part II-Section 2 of the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette,
dated the 12th May 2010, the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby
revises the minimum rates of wages payable to the classes
of employees in the employment in Medical and Sales
Representatives in the State of Tamil Nadu specified in column
(2) of the Schedule below, as specified in the corresponding
entries in column (3) thereof:-
THE SCHEDULE
Employment in Medical and Sales Representatives
Serial
Classes of employees
Minimum rates
Number
of basic wages
per month
(Rs.P.)
(1)
(2)

1.
Medical and Sales
8166.00
Representatives in
pharmaceutical manufacturing
or marketing units.
2.
Salesmen in
7017.00
Pharmaceutical wholesale
or distributor units.
Explanations.- (1) Dearness Allowance.-In addition to the
minimum rates of basic wages fixed above, the employees
shall be paid dearness allowance as indicated below:-
(i)
The dearness allowance is linked to the Average
Chennai City Consumer Price Index Number for the
year 2010, that is 161 points (with base 2001=100)
and for every rise of one point over and above 161
points, an increase of Rs.43.55 (Rupees forty three
and paise fifty five only) per point per month shall
be paid as dearness allowance.
(ii)
The dearness allowance shall be calculated every
year on the first April on the basis of the average
of the indices for the proceeding twelve months,
namely, from January to December.
(iii) The first calculation of the dearness allowance shall
thus be effective from the date of publication of this
Notification in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette,
based on the average of Chennai City Consumer
Price Index Number for the previous year.
(2) Where the nature of work is the same, no distinction
in payment of wages shall be made between men and women
employees.
(3) To arrive at daily wages, the monthly wages shall be
divided by 26.
(4) Wherever the existing wages are higher than the
minimum wages fixed herein, the same shall be continued to
be paid.

Explanations.- (1) Dearness Allowance.-In addition to the
above minimum rates of basic wages, the employees shall be
paid dearness allowance as follows:-
(i)
The dearness allowance shall be  linked to the Average
Consumer Price Index Number for Chennai City  for
the year   2000 that is 475 points (with base 1982=100)
and for every rise of one point over and above 475
points an increase of Rs.8.60 (Rupees Eight and
paise sixty  only) per month   shall be paid as
dearness allowance.
(ii)
The dearness allowance shall be calculated from the
first   April  of the every year on basis of the average
of the indices of the  proceeding twelve months, that
is from  January to December.
(iii) The  revision shall be  effective from the date of
publication of this Notification in the Tamil Nadu
Government Gazette, based on the average
Consumer Price Index of the previous year.
(2) Where the nature of work is the same, no distinction
in the payment of wages shall be made in the case of  men
and women employees.
(3) Where piece rate workers are employed in any public
motor transport, the remuneration paid to each of them for a
normal working day shall not be less than the minimum wages
fixed for appropriate category.
(4) To arrive at the daily  wages, the monthly wages shall
be devided by 26.
(5) The ‘Wages’ as defined in clause (h) of Section 2 of
the Minimum Wages Act, 1948 (Central Act XI of 1948) shall
be the criteria for the purpose of compliance of this Notification.
(6) Wherever the existing wages are higher than the
minimum wages fixed herein, such existing wages shall be
continued to be paid.

Explanation.—(1) Dearness Allowance.-In addition to the
minimum rates of basic wages fixed above, the employees
shall be paid dearness allowance as indicated below:—
(i)
The dearness allowance is linked to the Average
Consumer Price Index of Chennai City for the year
2010, that is 161 points with base 2001=100 any
further and for rise of every one point over and above
161 points, an increase of 95 paise per point (Ninety
five paise only) per day shall be paid as dearness
allowance.
(ii)
The dearness allowance shall be calculated every
year on the first April on the basic of the consumer
price indices for the preceding twelve month, that is
from January to December.
(iii)
The first calculation of the dearness allowance shall
thus be effective from the date of publication of this
Notification in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette
based on the Average of Chennai City Consumer
Price Index for the previous year.
(2) Where the nature of work is the same, no distinction
in the payment of wages shall be made between men and
women employees.
(3) To arrive at  Monthly rates of wages shall be multiplied
by 30.
(4) Wherever the existing wages are higher than the
minimum  wages fixed herein, the same shall be continued
to be paid.

Explanation.-(1) The above revised minimum rates of wages
shall also apply to the agricultural labourers employed in Colleges
and Research Station under the Tamil Nadu Agricultural
University and Agricultural Farms maintained by the Agriculture,
Horticulture and other Government Departments.

performed, no distinction in the payment of wages should be
made between men and women workers as per the Equal
Remuneration Act, 1976 (Central Act 25 of 1976).

wages specified above shall be all inclusive of rate allowing
for the basic rate, cost of living allowance and the cash value
of concession, if any, but it does not include the cost of food,
if any, supplied to the  workers and hence the cost of food
shall not be deducted from the minimum rates of wages paid
to the workers.

Explanation.—(1) Dearness Allowance.-In addition to the
minimum rates of basic wages fixed as above, the employees
shall be paid Dearness Allowance as indicated below:-
(i)
The Dearness Allowance is linked to the Average
Chennai City Consumer Price Index Number for the
year 2000, that is 475 points (with base 2001=100) and
for any further raise of every one point over and above
475 points, an increase of Rs. 5.20 (Rupees five and
paise twenty only) per month shall be paid as
Dearness Allowances.
(ii)
The Dearness Allowances shall be calculated every
year on the first April on the basic of the average of
the indices for the preceding twelve month, that is from
January to December.
(iii)
The first calculation of the Dearness Allowance shall
thus be effective from the date of publication of this
Notification in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette
based on the Average Chennai City Consumer Price
Index for the previous year.
(2) Classification of Zones shall be as follows:—
(i)
Zone A
-
shall include Municipal Corporation
and Special Grade Municipalities.
(ii)
Zone B
-
shall include all Municipalities other
than Special Grade Municipalities.
(iii)
Zone C
-
shall include Township, Town
Panchayats and Cantonments.
(iv)
Zone D
-
shall include all places other than
those 
mentioned 
in 
Zone
A, B and C.
(3) Where the same work or work of a similar nature is
performed by women, no distinction in the payment of wages
shall be made between men and women employees.
(4) To arrive at the daily wages, the monthly wages
shall be divided by 26.
(5) Wherever the existing wages are higher than the
minimum wages fixed herein, the same shall be continued
to be paid.

ENVIRONMENT AND FOREST DEPARTMENT
Declaration of Devarayasamudram, Forest Block Bit-I in
Namakkal Taluk and District as Reserved Forest under
the Tamil Nadu Forest Act.
Amendment to Notification
[G.O. Ms. No. 1, Environment and Forests (FR.14),
8th January 2014, ñ£˜èN 24, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-
2044.]
No. II(2)/EF/109/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 14 of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882 (Tamil Nadu
Act V of 1882), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby makes the
following amendment to the G.O. (Ms.) No. 159, Forest and
Fisheries (FR-3) Department, dated 25-02-1986. Notification
No. II(2)/FR.F1/3586/86 on page 429 of part II—Section 2 of
the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette dated 4th June 1986.
AMENDMENT
In the said notification for the expression “Personal Assistant
to the District Collector, Namakkal”, “Personal Assistant
(General) to the District Collector, Namakkal”, Shall be
substituted.
MOHAN VERGHESE CHUNKATH,
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.
